\eng{ij, uj.}}

\bentry
\word[jack(1)]{jack}
\pron{jAYxkf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{jAYxku: 

\alnum{a} etutxga; BAra etutxva yaMtarx. 

\alnum{b} Ure etutxga; vAhanada cakarxvanunx cokakxTa mADalu 
yA badalAyisalu acacxnunx meVletitx hiDiyuva salakaraNe, 
etutxva sAdhana. \quad
\hyperlink{jackfigure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width
    0.8cm height 0.6cm {J_Pictures/jack.jpg}}}

\alnum{c} gaDiyAradalilx gaMTeyanunx 
bArisuva, mAnavAkArada boMbe. 

\alnum{d} meVTukaDiDx; hApfRsikADfR modalAda vAdayxgaLalilx 
taMtiyanunx miDiyalu aLavaDisiruva salakaraNe. 

\alnum{e} \eng{ =
\hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cheapjack(1)}{${}^1$cheapjack}.}  

\alnum{f} \eng{ =
\hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{lumberjack}{lumberjack}.}  

\alnum{g} \eng{=
\hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{steeplejack}{steeplejack}}.  

\alnum{h} halavu yaMtarx modalAdavugaLa BAgagaLa hesaru. 

\alnum{i} \eng{ = \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bootjack}{bootjack}}. 

\alnum{j} (muMtAda cikakx athavA puTaTx) peYkf miVnu.

\alnum{k} (boVlfsx ATa) (ATagAraru guriyiDabeVkAda) puTaTx biLi ceMDu. 

\alnum{l} (\bava dalilx, \Eva vAgi parxyoVga) kalilxna athavA loVhada saNaNx 
goVligaLiMda ADuva oMdu ATa. 

\alnum{m} (kelavu jAti pArxNigaLalilx) gaMDupArxNi. 

\alnum{n} (\ashi) patetxVdAra; poliVsinavanu. 

\alnum{o} (\ame) (\ashi) haNa. 

\alnum{p} gulAma; manuSayxna, muKayxvAgi seYnikana, poVSAku toTiTxruva
 seVvaka, \mo vara  citarxviruva isipxVTele. 

\alnum{q} viduyxnamxMDalavanunx saMpakiRsuva sAdhana. 

\alnum{r} \eng{(Jack) (John} eMbudara badalu baLasuva \rUpa) 
shirxVsAmAnayx athavA yAvudeV jAtiya
pArxNiya gaMDu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{everyman jack} parxtiyobabxnU; parxtiyobabx
gaMDasU.
\num{2} \eng{Jack and Jill} 

\alnum{a} poVrapoVri; huDuga huDugi. 

\alnum{b} gaMDu heNuNx; gaMDasu heMgasu. 
\num{3} \eng{jack of all trades} sakala 
kAyaRpaTu; savaRkAyaR nipuNa; elalx kelasagaLanUnx mADabalalxvanu; yAvudeV 
kasubu mADabalalxvanu.}} 

\noindent
\gl{\nuga} 
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{before you could say Jack Robinson} 
`jAyxkf rAbinfsanf' enunxvaSaTxralilxyeV, enunxvaSaTxkUkx muMceyeV; bahaLa beVgane athavA kUDaleV. 
\num{2} \eng{on one's jack (\engit{also}, on one's Jack Jones)} (\ashi) oMTiyAgi; obobxMTiganAgi.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[jam(1)]{jam}
\pron{jAYxmf}
\gl{\kirx} (\vakaq\ \eng{jamming}, \BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{jammed}).
{\dictmeaning{}} 

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (eraDu talagaLa madheyx vasutxvanunx) amuku; jaDi; turuku; iruku; aDaku. 
\num{2} (yaMtarx BAgavanunx) kelasakekx bAradaMte -- irukisu, adumi biDu, jajijx biDu. 
\num{3} yaMtarxvanunx adumi biTuTx kelasa mADadaMte mADu. 
\num{4} (vasutxgaLu otAtxgi mudedxyAguvaMte) adumu; giDi. 
\num{5} (vasutxvanunx, ikakxTuTx jAga \mo vugaLa oLakekx) balavAgi -- taLuLx, 
turuku, nUku, giDi, jaDi. 
\num{6} (mAgaR \mo vanunx) kikikxridu tuMbi, neredu, seVri -- aDacibiDu, baMdf mADi biDu.
\eng{7} (reVDiyoV) adumu; iruku; saMmadiRsu (samAna taraMgAMtaradalilx 
reVDiyoV alegaLanunx parxsAra mADi anayxra reVDiyoV athavA reVDArf saMkeVtagaLanunx) gajibiji mADu. 
\num{8} nigaRmanavanunx -- taDe, niroVdhisu: \eng{we were jammed in}
horabaradaMte namamxnunx taDeyalAyitu. 
\num{9} (\sA\ \eng{jam on}) (berxVkugaLu \mo vugaLanunx) balavaMtavAgi athavA idadxkikxdadxMte -- amuku, 
hAku, otutx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} (beNe hAkidaMte) bigiyAgi sikikxko, irukiko, aDaciko. 
\num{2} (yaMtarxda \vi) yaMtarxda BAgavu aDaci(koMDiruvudariMda) kelasa mADadaMte Agiru.
\num{3} (jAyxsf \saM). (\AmA) (hosa layagatigaLanunx seVrisikoLuLxtAtx) samaya
sUPxtiRyiMda hADu; tatAkxlada utAsxhadiMda hADu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[join(1)]{join}
\pron{jAinf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (vasutxgaLanunx oMdanonxMdakekx, oTiTxge) kUDisu; seVrisu; 
jaMTihAku; saMyoVjisu; joVDisu; baMdhisu. 
\num{2} (eraDu biMdugaLanunx) (\kanmu\ saraLa) reVKeyiMda -- seVrisu, kUDisu. 
\num{3} (vayxkitxgaLanunx maduve, senxVha, bAMdhavayx, \mo vugaLa mUlaka) 
oMdAgisu; oTuTxgUDisu; oMdugUDisu; (vayxkitxgaLalilx parasapxra) saMbaMdha uMTumADu. 
\num{4} (obabx vayxkitxya) oDanADiyAgu; jote seVru; jotegUDu; sahavAsa seVru. 
\num{5} (kelasa, BoVjana, \mo vugaLalilx vayxkitxya) jotege seVru; oDane BAgiyAgu. 
\num{6} (saMGa, seYnayx, \mo vugaLa) sadasayxnAgu; sadasayxnAgi seVru. 
\num{7} (seYnayxpaDe, haDagu, vANijayx saMsethx, \mo vugaLalilx) tananx sAthxnakekx, 
hudedxge, seVriko athavA tananx sAthxnavanunx punavaRhisiko. 
\num{8} kUDu; seVriko; saMgamavAgu; saMgamisu: {\eng{the Kapila \eng{join}s the 
Kaveri at Tirumakudala Narasipur}} tirumakUDalu narasiVpuradalilx kapilA nadiyu kAveVriyanunx 
seVrikoLuLxtatxde. kapilA nadiyu kAveVriyoDane saMgamisutatxde.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} oMdugUDu; oMdAgu; oTuTxgUDu; EkiVBavisu. 
\num{2} (mADuvudaralilx athavA kAyaRdalilx) itararoDane -- seVriko, BAgavahisu, BAgiyAgu, pAlogxLuLx.}}

\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{

\alnum{b} parasapxra keY keY joVDisu. 

\alnum{c} (\rUpa) (oMdu kAyaRdalilx athavA udayxmadalilx) oMdugUDu; oMdAgu; oTATxgi seVru; saMyoVga hoMdu.

\alnum{a} (vivAdAMshaveMdu opipxda viSayada meVle, inonx\-babxroDane) vAdakekx -- iLi, toDagu, AraMBisu: \eng{we shall be ready to join issue with them on this very point} nAvu avaroDane I aMshada meVleyeV vAda mADalu sidadhx.

\bentry
\word[judge(1)]{judge}
\pron{jajf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} jaDijx; jaDujx; nAyxyAdhipati; nAyxyAdhiVsha; nAyxyamUtiR. 
\num{2} (deVvara \vi) atuyxnanxta nAyxyamUtiR, tiVpuRgAra:
\eng{God is my judge} deVvareV nanage tiVpuRgAra. 
\num{3} 
\alnum{a} (yehUdayx \ca) jaDujx; joVSuana taruvAya rAjara ALivxke
baruvavaregina madhayxkAladalilx, iserxVlinalilx tAtAkxlikavAgi
adhikAra naDesutitxdadx adhikAri. 

\alnum{b} (\bava dalilx) jaDfjx; I avadhiya cariterxyanonxLagoMDa, 
beyxbalfna haLeya oDaMbaDikeya ELaneya pusatxka. 
\num{4} tiVpuRgAra; paMcAyita(dAra); vivAda, paMdayx, \mo
vugaLalilx tiVpuR koDalu niyamitanAdavanu athavA avugaLanunx
bageharisuvavanu, itayxthaR mADuvavanu. 
\num{5} tiVpuRgAra; yAvudeV samaseyxyanunx bageharisuvavanu. 
\num{6} (yoVgayxteya) niNaRyakAra;
tiVpuRgAra; vasutxvina athavA samaseyxya balAbalagaLanunx,
yoVgayxteyanunx, guNAvaguNagaLanunx, tiVmARnisalu dakaSxnAdavanu:
\eng{I am no judge of diamonds}  nAnu vajarxgaLa guNAvaguNagaLananxrita tiVpuRgAranalalx.}
\eentry


\bentry
\word[judge(2)]{judge}
\pron{jajf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (nAyxyAladalilx obabxna athavA oMdara meVle) tiVpuR koDu. 
\num{2} (vayxvahAravanunx, mokadadxmeyanunx) vicAraNe mADu. 
\num{3} (oMdu viSayavanunx) tiVmARnisu; niNaRyisu. 
\num{4}(--eMbudAgi) tiVpuR koDu; vidhisu; vidhAyaka mADu. 
\num{5} (\kanmu\ yehUdayx \ca) (joVSuana taruvAya rAjara ALivxke baruvavaregina madhayxkAladalilx iserxVlinalilx) tAtAkxlikavAgi
ADaLita naDesu. 
\num{6} tiVpuRkoDu; tiVmARnisu; bageharisu; itayxthaR mADu. 
\num{7} (obabxna yoVgayxteya \vi\ avana kaqtayx \mo vugaLiMda)
yoVgayxte niNaRyisu; aBipArxya taLe. 
\num{8} (\pArxparx) TiVkisu; AkeSxVpisu; KaMDisu: 
\eng{judge not that ye be not judged} ninanxnunx (itararu KaMDisadiruva saluvAgi niVnU
avaranunx) KaMDisadiru. 
\num{9} (aMkiaMshagaLiMda oMdu vasutxvina yA
viSayada savxrUpada bagegx) tiVmARnakekx baru; tiVmARnisu;
niNaRyisu.

\bentry
\word{judgement}
\pron{jajfmaMTf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (nAyxyAlayada, nAyxyAdhiVshana) tiVpuR; koVTiRna tiVmARna, niNaRya. 
\num{2} deYvashApa; deYva shikeSx; BagavaMtana asamAdhAnada
PalaveMdu BAvisuva keVDu, duradaqSaTx, saMkaTa, vipatutx (kelavomemx \hA): 
\eng{it is a judgement on you for getting up late}
hotAtxgi edadx tapipxgAgi ninage BagavaMta koTaTx shikeSx. 
\num{3} TiVke; KaMDane. 
\num{4} aBipArxya; BAvane: \eng{in my judgement} nananx aBipArxyadalilx, 
BAvaneyalilx. 
\num{5} vimashaRna shakitx; viveVcana shakitx. 
\num{6} viveVcane; aucitayx parxjecnx; yukAtxyukatx parijAcnxna.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{against one's better judgement} tananx
viveVcanege vayxtirikatxvAgi; tananx yukAtxyukatx -- viveVkakekx, 
parijAcnxnakekx, virudadhxvAgi. 
\num{2} \eng{day of judgement (\engit{also} Judgement Day)} aMtima tiVpiRna
dina; parxlayada taruvAya deVvaru naDesuva mahAvicAraNeya
dina.  
\num{3} \eng{Judgement of Paris} (\girxVpu) pAyxrisana
tiVpuR; swMdayaR sapxdheRyalilx pAyxrisanu cinanxda seVbanunx
aphorxditege koTiTxdudx (idu helenaLa apaharaNakekx, adariMdAgi
TorxVjanf yudadhxkekx kAraNavAyitu). 
\num{4} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{sit(1) pagu(12)}{${}^1$sit} in judgement} (itarara meVle) vimasheRge kUru; (itararanunx, itarara guNadoVSagaLanunx) TiVkisu; dUSisu; 
itarara yoVgayxte, naDate, \mo vugaLanunx niNaRyisi tiVpuR koDuva adhikAravanunx vahisu.
\num{5} \eng{the Last J{udgement}} aMtima tiVpuR; (elalx jiVvarugaLigU 
avara aihika jiVvanadalilx mADida pApa
puNayxgaLige takakxMte) parxpaMcada aMtayxdalilx deVvaru niVDuva mahA
tiVmARna.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{judicially}
\pron{jU(ju)DiSali}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} nAyxyikavAgi 

\alnum{a} nAyxya niNaRyadaMte. 

\alnum{b} nAyxyAdhipatiya adhikArada parxkAra.

\pron{jaMboV}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{%
(\bava\ \eng{jumbos}). 
\num{1} doDaDx gAtarxda, BAri -- manuSayx athavA pArxNi athavA vasutx (\kanmu\ Ane). 
\num{2} (\kanmu) laMDaninxna maqgAlayada `jaMboV' eMba hesarina viKAyxta Ane. 
\num{3} mahatAsxdhaka; BAri sAdhaneyava; baduku matutx kAyaRgaLalilx gamana
seLeyuvaMte saPalate paDedavanu. 
\num{4} (yAvudaradeV) BAri mAdari; bahaLa doDaDx mAdari. 
\num{5} \eng{= \hyperlink{jumbo jet}{jumbo jet}}.}
\eentry



\bentry

\bentry
\word[jump(1)]{jump}
\pron{jaMpf }
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} (neladiMda) negeta; eguru; hArike; cimumxvike; kupapxLike;
kupapxLa; laMGana. 
\num{2} becicx biVLuvudu;  hwhAruvudu; cakitagoLuLxvudu; saMBarxma, 
duguDa athavA AGAtadiMda Aguva becucx. 
\num{3} (mobalagu, bele, dara, mwlayx, \mo vugaLa) thaTaTxneya
Erike; haThAtf hecacxLa; Akasimxka teVji. 
\num{4} EkAEkiya badalAvaNe; haThAtf parivataRne. 
\num{5} laMGana; hArike; negeta; atikarxmaNa;
saraNi, vAda, \mo vugaLalilx anukarxmavAgi muMduvareyade,
idadxkikxdadxMte naDuvaNa haMtagaLanunx, GaTaTxgaLanunx atikarxmisi
hArida aMtara. 
\num{6} (kudure \mo vu) hArabeVkAgiruva -- aDiDx, aDacaNe. 
\num{7} \eng{= \hyperlink{jump bid}{jump bid}}. 
\num{8} \eng{= \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{ski-jump}{ski-jump}.}}} 

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{\eng{the jumps} (\ashi) 

\alnum{a} (ati kuDitadiMdAguva) kaMpana saninx(pAta); ede naDuka;
haqdayakaMpana.  

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) ede naDuka; ede DavaguTuTxvudu; haqdayakaMpana; 
parxbalaBiVti: \eng{this place fairly gives me the jumps} 
I jAga nanage ede naDuka huTiTxsutatxde, barisutatxde.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{get the jump on (\engit{also}, have the jump on)} (\ashi)
(edurALiya hUTavanunx muninxriVkiSxsi avananunx) miVrisuva -- avakAsha
paDe, dorakisiko.  
\num{2} \eng{one jump ahead} (edurALiya hUTa,
taMtarxgaLanunx muninxriVkiSxsi avanigiMta ) oMdu hejejx muMdAda; oMdu
dATu muMde hoVda. 
\num{3} \eng{on the jump} (\AmA) saDagaradiMda, saMBarxmadiMda --
ODADutAtx.}
\eentry


\bentry
\word[jump(2)]{jump}
\pron{jaMpf }
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} (hebAbxgilu \mo vanunx) hAru; hAri dATu; laMGisu. 
\num{2} (vAhanada \vi) (keMpu saMkeVta diVpavanunx kaDegaNisi) dATu;
mununxgugx; muMde -- sAgu, hAdu hoVgu. 
\num{3} (reYlu, TArxYxmf, \mo vugaLa \vi) kaMbi(yanunx), 
haLi(yanunx) -- tapupx; kaMbi(yanunx) biTuTxhoVgu. 
\num{4} (aDaDx baMda vasutxvanunx) hAru; dATu; negedu muMde hoVgu. 
\num{5} (\ame) (reYlu \mo vanunx athavA \mo vugaLiMda \kanmu\
kAnUnige virudadxvAda riVtiyalilx) thaTaTxne hatutx athavA iLi. 
\num{6} (opapxMda, hoNe, \mo vanunx) muri; keYbiDu; tore; BaMgamADu. 
\num{7} (magu \mo varige) keLakekx hAralu neravAgu; dumukalu sahAya mADu. 
\num{8} (vasutxvanunx athavA pArxNiyanunx, \kanmu\ kudureyanunx)
hArisu; negesu; jigisu; cimimxsu. 
\num{9} hAralu, negeyalu (kudureyanunx) baLasu; 
kudureyanenxVri (yAvudara meVlAgali) hAru. 
\num{10} (\sA\ \BUkaq dalilx) (AlUgeDeDx \mo vanunx bANaleyalilx
AgAga) kedakutatx -- kari, huri, bADisu. 
\num{11} (vayxkitxya, vasutxvina meVle) eragu; eguribiVLu. 
\num{12} (vidhisida kAlakekx) muMceyeV mADibiDu. 
\num{13} (hiMdina anuBavadAranu toredu biTiTxdedxMba athavA 
kAyideyaMte kaLedukoMDaneMba nevadiMda avana hakakxnunx, kAyide
karxmakekx kAyade) sarakakxne vashapaDisiko; AturadiMda
Akarxmisiko. 
\num{14} (viSaya, pusatxkada BAga, \mo vanunx kaNuNx
hAyisutAtx)  dATi hoVgu; hArisi biDu. 
\num{15} (baMDeyanunx, baMDeyalilx tUtanunx) monacu gaDAriyiMda kore. 
\num{16} (beleyanunx) idadxkikxdadxMte -- Erisu, hecicxsu, EruvaMte mADu. 
\num{17} (madhayxdalilxna vasutxvanunx biTuTx, muMde) hoVgu; dATu; hAru.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (nela \mo vugaLiMda meVlakekx) nege; eguru; hAru;
cimumx; jigi; kupapxLisu; laMGisu. 
\num{2} (miVnina \vi) bAlavanunx nimirisi cimumx. 
\num{3} (Asana \mo vugaLiMda meVlakekx, etatxrada
sathxLadiMda dUrakekx) nege; hAru; jigi: \eng{we jumped up}
nAvu meVlakekx negedevu. 
\num{4} (saMBarxma, duguDa, AGAta, \mo vugaLiMda) thaTaTxne --
becicxbiVLu, negedADu, kuNidADu: (\kanmu)
\eng{jump for joy} saMtoVSadiMda negedADu, kuNidADu. 
\num{5} (bele \mo vugaLa \vi) idadxkikxdadxMte -- Eru, hecAcxgu: 
\eng{prices jumped} belegaLu haThAtatxne Eridavu. 
\num{6} AturadiMda tiVmARnakekx baru; tiVmARnakekx diDiVrane dhumuku. 
\num{7} idadxkikxdadxMte (pArxmuKayx, sAthxna, \mo vakekx) -- Eru, hAru, nege. 
\num{8} (obabxnoDanobabx, oMdaroDanoMdu) hoMdiko; hoMdAvaNege
baru; oMdAgu; meVLayisu. 
\num{9} oMdu BAvane athavA viSayadiMda inonxMdakekx -- hAru, egaru, 
nege, beVga hoVgu athavA badalAyisu. 
\num{10} idadxkikxdadxMte athavA AturAturavAgi nidiRSaTx riVtiyalilx calisu:
\eng{we jumped into the car} nAvu kArinoLakekx hAri
kuLitevu. \eng{jumped from (\engit{or} out of) the car} nAvu kAriniMda horakekx negedavu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{jump in} (gADi \mo vugaLoLakekx) curukAgi hAriko. 
\num{2} \eng{jump the queue} (\birx) kUyx hAru; sAlu
hAru; paMkitx laMGisu; kUyxnalilx niMtidadxvaranunx hiMdakekx hAki
muMdakekx hoVgu, muMde hoVgi nilulx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{jump at} (\rUpa) (vAgAdxna, lABada
vAyxpAra, \mo vanunx) tavakadiMda, tavxreyiMda, AturadiMda -- opipxko,
aMgiVkarisu, hiDiduko. 
\hyperdef{J}{jump(2) nuga(2)}{}
\num{2} \eng{jump down person's throat} 

\alnum{a} obabxnanunx birusAgi KaMDisu, CiVmAri hAku. 

\alnum{b} obabxnige birusAgi parxtuyxtatxra koDu. 
\num{3} \eng{jump in the lake} (\AmA) (\sA\ vidhi 
rUpadalilx) tolagi hoVgu; hoVgi kerege biVLu. 
\num{4} \eng{jump on (or upon)} (mAtiniMda athavA kAyaRdiMda) 
huTaTxDagisu; taleetatxdaMte meVleragu; meVle bidudx
tuLidu hAku (\rUpa\ saha). 
\num{5} \eng{jump on the bandwagon} gelulxva pakaSx hiDi; 
gelulxvetitxna bAla hiDi; yashasivxyAguvaMtiruvavara kaDe seVriko. 
\num{6} \eng{jump out of one's \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{skin(1) pagu(4)}{${}^1$skin}} (AshacxyaR, AnaMda, \mo vugaLiMda) becicxbiVLu; hwhAru; cakitanAgu. 
\num{7} \eng{jump over the broomstick} maduve mADiko; vivAhavAgu. 
\num{8} \eng{jump ship} (nAvikana \vi) (mADikoMDiruva opapxMdada 
avadhi mugiyuvudakikxMta muMceyeV) kelasavanunx toredu hoVgu. 
\num{9} \eng{jump the gun} (\AmA) siganxlf koDuvudakekx muMce 
yA opipxda kAlakekx -- horaDu. 
\num{10} \eng{jump together} oMdaroDanoMdu pUtiRyAgi meVLayisu, hoMdiko. 
\num{11} \eng{jump to it} adakekx athavA kelasakekx dhumuku; kUDaleV 
birusiniMda pArxraMBisu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[jumper(1)]{jumper}
\pron{jaMparf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{%
\num{1} jaMparu; laMGaka: 

\alnum{a} negeyuvavanu athavA negeyuva pArxNi. 

\alnum{b} hAruva kiVTa, \udA\ cigaTa. 
\num{2} (hiMdina anuBavadAranu toredubiTaTxneMba athavA kAyideyaMte kaLedukoMDaneMba
nevadiMda, oMdu hakakxnunx, kAnUnu karxmakekx kAyade) sarakakxne
vashapaDisikoLuLxvavanu. 
\num{3} jaMparu; monacu -- gaDAri athavA beYrige; baMDe \mo vanunx oDeyalu 
siDimadudx tuMbuvudakAkxgi tUtu koreyalu
baLasuva, uLiyalagina, BAravAda gaDAri athavA beYrige. 
\num{4} laMGana paMthi; ArAdhaneya oMdu aMgavAgi negeyutitxdadx athavA negeyuva veVlisxna
methaDisfTx paMthadavanu athavA anaMtarada beVre paMthagaLavanu. 
\num{5} bigi horaji; hAyikaMba, kovemara, aDaDxdUla, jaMti, \mo vu
alAlxDadaMte bigidu kaTuTxva horaji, dapapx hagagx. 
\num{6} (\viduyx) jaMparu; viduyxnamxMDalavanunx kUDisuva 
yA beVpaRDisuva tuMDu taMti.}
\eentry

\num{2} hAri dATuva. 
\num{3} (saMtoVSa \mo vugaLiMda) negedADuva; kuNiyuva. 
\num{4} (bele \mo vu idadxkikxdadxMte) Eri biDuva; teVjiyAguva. 
\num{5} (vAda \mo vugaLalilx) Aturada tiVmARnakekx -- negeyuva, 
dhumukuva, hAribiDuva. 
\num{6} (girAkiyu koDalopipxda beleyanunx athavA opipxge 
haMta muTiTxda vAyxpAravanunx) AturadiMda opipxkoLuLxva. 
\num{7} (tapipxtasathx \mo vara meVle bidudx, avara huTaTxDagisuvaMte) 
hAri biVLuva; eragi biVLuva. 
\num{8} (oMdaroDanoMdu) hoMdikoLuLxva; meVLayisuva. 
\num{9} (hebAbxgilu \mo vanunx) hAruva, hAri dATuva. 
\num{10} (reYlevx baMDiya \vi) kaMbi, haLi -- tapupxva. 
\num{11} (magu \mo vanunx) negesuva athavA dhumukisuva. 
\num{12} (vasutxvanunx) hArisuva; negesuva; cimimxsuva; jigisuva. 
\num{13} (vayxkitxyanunx) becicx biVLisuva; hwhArisuva. 
\num{14} (AlUgeDeDx \mo vanunx) bANaleyalilx AgAga
	kedakutatx kariyuva. 
\num{15} (itararanunx, avarige tiLiyadaMteyeV) atikarxmisuva. 
\num{16} (hiMdina anuBavadAranu toredaneMba athavA kAyideyaMte 
	kaLedukoMDaneMba nevadiMda, oMdu hakakxnunx, kAyide 
	karxmakekx kAyade) sarakakxne
	kasidukoLuLxva.

	kaNuNx hAyisutAtx) hArisibiDuva.}

\bentry
\word{jungle}
\pron{jaMga(gf)lf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (\kanmu\ uSaNxvalayagaLalilxna) kADu; kAnu; jaMgalu; aDavi;
araNayx; vana; kurucalu beLeda athavA maragaLu daTaTxvAgi beLeda BUmi. 
\num{2} kADu BUmi; araNayx parxdeVsha. 
\num{3} jiVvana saMgArxma raMga; uLivigAgi naDeyuva kUrxra hoVrATada parxdeVsha. 
\num{4} kupepx; asatxvayxsatx rAshi; avayxvasithxta guDeDx; karxmavilalxde sikAkxpaTeTx oTuTxgUDisiruva rAshi: 
\eng{a jungle of files} daphatxragaLa kADu, asatxvayxsatx rAshi. 
\num{5} kADu; dikukx toVcadaMte mADuva athavA goMdalamayavAgiruva
parxdeVsha: \eng{blackboard jungle in schools} shAlegaLalilxna
kapupxhalage kADu. \eng{concrete jungle in cities}
nagaragaLalilxna kAMkirxVTu (kaTaTxDagaLa) kADu. 
\num{6} hiMsAraMga athavA sapxdhARraMga; hiMsAcArada athavA nidaRya sapxdheRya parxdeVsha.}}

\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{common jury} sAmAnayx nAyxyadashiR
maMDali; sAdhAraNA vagaRda vayxkitxgaLu sadasayxrAgiruva nAyxyadashiR maMDali.

pariVkiSxsalu neVmisida vayxkitxgaLa maMDali.

\eng{(wait) just a minute, please} dayaviTuTx oMdeV

avananunx Iga tAneV noVDide.

aSeTx. \eng{we are just good friends} nAvu oLeLxya senxVhitaru
aSeTx. \eng{it just doesn't make sense} adaralelxVnU,

\num{10} saMpUNaRvAgi; pUtiRyAgi; savaRthA: \eng{not just yet} inUnx
